      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government">
        Government
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Government">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Aruba" title="Politics of Aruba">
        Politics of Aruba
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1358" data-file-width="2206" height="135" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png/220px-EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png/330px-EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png/440px-EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:EU_OCT_and_OMR_map_en.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Map of the European Union in the world with overseas countries and territories and outermost regions
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Willem-Alexander,_Prince_of_Orange.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2386" data-file-width="2000" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg/170px-Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg/255px-Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg/340px-Willem-Alexander%2C_Prince_of_Orange.jpg 2x" width="170"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Willem-Alexander,_Prince_of_Orange.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Willem-Alexander_of_the_Netherlands" title="Willem-Alexander of the Netherlands">
          King Willem-Alexander
         </a>
         is the
         <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">
          head of state
         </a>
         of Aruba
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Parlamentodiaruba.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1654" data-file-width="2539" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Parlamentodiaruba.jpg/220px-Parlamentodiaruba.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Parlamentodiaruba.jpg/330px-Parlamentodiaruba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Parlamentodiaruba.jpg/440px-Parlamentodiaruba.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Parlamentodiaruba.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Parliament of Aruba in
         <a href="/wiki/Oranjestad,_Aruba" title="Oranjestad, Aruba">
          Oranjestad
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       As a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Countries_of_the_Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Countries of the Kingdom of the Netherlands">
        constituent country
       </a>
       of the
       <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">
        Kingdom of the Netherlands
       </a>
       , Aruba's politics take place within a framework of a 21-member
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parliamentary_democracy" title="Parliamentary democracy">
        Parliament
       </a>
       and an eight-member Cabinet. The
       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Aruba" title="Governor of Aruba">
        governor of Aruba
       </a>
       is appointed for a six-year term by the monarch, and the prime minister and deputy prime minister are elected by the Staten (or "Parlamento") for four-year terms. The Staten is made up of 21 members elected by direct, popular vote to serve a four-year term.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
        <a href="#cite_note-18">
         [18]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Together with the
       <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">
        Netherlands
       </a>
       , the countries of Aruba,
       <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaçao">
        Curaçao
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Sint_Maarten" title="Sint Maarten">
        Sint Maarten
       </a>
       form the
       <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">
        Kingdom of the Netherlands
       </a>
       . As they share the same Dutch citizenship, these four countries still also share the Dutch passport as the Kingdom of the Netherlands passport. As Aruba, Curaçao and Sint Maarten have small populations, the three countries had to limit immigration. To protect their population, they have the right to control the admission and expulsion of people from the Netherlands.
      </p>
      <p>
       Aruba is designated as a member of the Overseas Countries and Territories (OCT) and is thus officially not a part of the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       , though Aruba can and does receive support from the European Development Fund.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-euprofile_19-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-euprofile-19">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
        <a href="#cite_note-20">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Politics">
        Politics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Politics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The Aruban legal system is based on the Dutch model. In Aruba, legal jurisdiction lies with the
       <i>
        Gerecht in Eerste Aanleg
       </i>
       (
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Court_of_First_Instance" title="Court of First Instance">
        Court of First Instance
       </a>
       ) on Aruba, the
       <i>
        Gemeenschappelijk Hof van Justitie van Aruba, Curaçao, Sint Maarten en van Bonaire, Sint Eustatius en Saba
       </i>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Court_of_Justice_of_Aruba,_Cura%C3%A7ao,_Sint_Maarten,_and_of_Bonaire,_Sint_Eustatius_and_Saba" title="Joint Court of Justice of Aruba, Curaçao, Sint Maarten, and of Bonaire, Sint Eustatius and Saba">
        Joint Court of Justice of Aruba, Curaçao, Sint Maarten, and of Bonaire, Sint Eustatius and Saba
       </a>
       ) and the
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hoge_Raad_der_Nederlanden" title="Hoge Raad der Nederlanden">
         Hoge Raad der Nederlanden
        </a>
       </i>
       (Supreme Court of Justice of the Netherlands).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
        <a href="#cite_note-21">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The
       <i>
        Korps Politie Aruba
       </i>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Aruba_Police_Force" title="Aruba Police Force">
        Aruba Police Force
       </a>
       ) is the island's law enforcement agency and operates district precincts in Oranjestad, Noord, San Nicolaas, and Santa Cruz, where it is headquartered.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KPA-districts_22-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-KPA-districts-22">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Deficit_spending" title="Deficit spending">
        Deficit spending
       </a>
       has been a staple in Aruba's history, and modestly high inflation has been present as well. By 2006, the government's debt had grown to 1.883 billion Aruban florins.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
        <a href="#cite_note-23">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Aruba received some
       <a href="/wiki/Development_aid" title="Development aid">
        development aid
       </a>
       from the Dutch government each year through 2009, as part of a deal (signed as "Aruba's Financial Independence") in which the Netherlands gradually reduced its financial help to the island each successive year.
      </p>
      <p>
       In 2006, the Aruban government changed several tax laws to reduce the deficit.
       <a href="/wiki/Direct_tax" title="Direct tax">
        Direct taxes
       </a>
       have been converted to indirect taxes as proposed by the
       <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">
        IMF
       </a>
       . A 3% tax has been introduced on sales and services, while income taxes have been lowered and revenue taxes for business reduced by 20%. The government compensated workers with 3.1% for the effect that the B.B.O. would have on the inflation for 2007.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">
        Education
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Education">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Aruba's educational system is patterned after the
       <a href="/wiki/Education_in_the_Netherlands" title="Education in the Netherlands">
        Dutch system of education
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bogaerts_(Transitional_times)_24-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Bogaerts_(Transitional_times)-24">
         [24]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The Government of Aruba finances the public national education system.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2015)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       There are private schools, including the
       <a href="/wiki/International_School_of_Aruba" title="International School of Aruba">
        International School of Aruba
       </a>
       and Schakel College.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2015)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       There are two
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Medical_schools" title="Medical schools">
        medical schools
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Aureus_University_School_of_Medicine" title="Aureus University School of Medicine">
        Aureus University School of Medicine
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Xavier_University_School_of_Medicine" title="Xavier University School of Medicine">
        Xavier University School of Medicine
       </a>
       ,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">
        <a href="#cite_note-25">
         [25]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">
        <a href="#cite_note-26">
         [26]
        </a>
       </sup>
       as well as its own national university, the University of Aruba.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">
        Economy
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Economy">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Aruba" title="Economy of Aruba">
        Economy of Aruba
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Aruba has one of the highest standards of living in the Caribbean region. There is a low unemployment rate.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">
        <a href="#cite_note-27">
         [27]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The GDP per capita for Aruba was estimated to be $28,924 in 2014; among the highest in the Caribbean and the Americas.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_16-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-16">
         [16]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Its main trading partners are Colombia, the United States, Venezuela, and the
       <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">
        Netherlands
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:372px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aruba_export_map.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="520" data-file-width="640" height="301" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Aruba_export_map.png/370px-Aruba_export_map.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Aruba_export_map.png/555px-Aruba_export_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/05/Aruba_export_map.png 2x" width="370"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aruba_export_map.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A graphical breakdown of Aruba's economy by exports
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The island's economy has been dominated by three main industries: tourism,
       <a href="/wiki/Aloe" title="Aloe">
        aloe
       </a>
       export, and
       <a href="/wiki/Oil_refinery" title="Oil refinery">
        petroleum refining
       </a>
       (The
       <a href="/wiki/Lago_Oil_and_Transport_Company" title="Lago Oil and Transport Company">
        Lago Oil and Transport Company
       </a>
       and the Arend Petroleum Maatschappij Shell Co.).
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       Before the "Status Aparte" (a separate completely autonomous country/state within the Kingdom), oil processing was the dominant industry in Aruba despite expansion of the tourism sector. Today, the influence of the oil processing business is minimal
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag needs further explanation. (February 2017)">
           further explanation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       . The size of the agriculture and manufacturing sectors also remains minimal.
      </p>
      <p>
       The official exchange rate of the
       <a href="/wiki/Aruban_florin" title="Aruban florin">
        Aruban florin
       </a>
       is pegged to the US dollar at 1.79 florins to 1 USD.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">
        <a href="#cite_note-28">
         [28]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
        <a href="#cite_note-29">
         [29]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Because of this fact, and due to a large number of American tourists, many businesses operate using US dollars instead of florins, especially in the hotel and resort districts.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">
        Tourism
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Tourism">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       About three quarters of the Aruban
       <a href="/wiki/Gross_national_product" title="Gross national product">
        gross national product
       </a>
       is earned through tourism or related activities.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CIA_30-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-CIA-30">
         [30]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Most tourists are from the United States (predominantly from the north-east US), the Netherlands and South America, mainly Venezuela and Colombia.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2013)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       As part of the Kingdom of the Netherlands, citizens of the Netherlands can travel with relative ease to Aruba and other islands of the Dutch Antilles. No visas are needed for Dutch citizens, only a passport, and although the currency used in Aruba is different (the Netherlands uses the
       <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">
        Euro
       </a>
       ), money can be easily exchanged at a local bank for
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aruban_Florin" title="Aruban Florin">
        Aruban Florins
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       For the facilitation of the passengers whose destination is the United States, the
       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Homeland_Security" title="United States Department of Homeland Security">
        United States Department of Homeland Security
       </a>
       (DHS),
       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Customs_and_Border_Protection" title="U.S. Customs and Border Protection">
        U.S. Customs and Border Protection
       </a>
       (CBP) full pre-clearance facility in Aruba has been in effect since 1 February 2001 with the expansion in the Queen Beatrix Airport. United States and Aruba have had the agreement since 1986. It began as a USDA and Customs post. Since 2008, Aruba has been the only island to have this service for private flights.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">
        <a href="#cite_note-31">
         [31]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Military">
        Military
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Military">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Aruba" title="Military of Aruba">
        Military of Aruba
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Defense on
       <i>
        Aruba
       </i>
       is the responsibility of the
       <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">
        Kingdom of the Netherlands
       </a>
       . The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_the_Netherlands" title="Military of the Netherlands">
        Netherlands Military
       </a>
       forces that protect
       <i>
        Aruba
       </i>
       include the
       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Netherlands_Navy" title="Royal Netherlands Navy">
        Royal Netherlands Navy
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Marine_Corps" title="Netherlands Marine Corps">
        Netherlands Marine Corps
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Coastguard" title="Netherlands Coastguard">
        Netherlands Coastguard
       </a>
       . There is also a small indigenous "Arubaanse Militie" (ARUMIL) of about platoon strength. All forces are stationed at Marines Barracks Savaneta. Furthermore, in 1999 the
       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">
        U.S. Department of Defense
       </a>
       established a
       <a href="/wiki/Forward_Operating_Site" title="Forward Operating Site">
        Forward Operating Location
       </a>
       (FOL) at the airport.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">
        <a href="#cite_note-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">
        Culture
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Culture">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Aruba" title="Culture of Aruba">
        Culture of Aruba
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Music_of_Aruba_and_the_Netherlands_Antilles" title="Music of Aruba and the Netherlands Antilles">
        Music of Aruba and the Netherlands Antilles
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="785" data-file-width="1188" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg/220px-Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg/330px-Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg/440px-Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Centrum_Oranjestad.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Ornate buildings in
         <a href="/wiki/Oranjestad,_Aruba" title="Oranjestad, Aruba">
          Oranjestad, Aruba
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       On 18 March, Aruba celebrates its National Day. In 1976, Aruba presented its National Anthem (Aruba Dushi Tera) and Flag.
      </p>
      <p>
       Aruba has a varied culture. According to the
       <i>
        Bureau Burgelijke Stand en Bevolkingsregister
       </i>
       (BBSB), in 2005 there were ninety-two different nationalities living on the island. Dutch influence can still be seen, as in the celebration of "
       <a href="/wiki/Sinterklaas" title="Sinterklaas">
        Sinterklaas
       </a>
       " on 5 and 6 December and other national holidays like 27 April, when in Aruba and the rest of the Kingdom of the Netherlands the King's birthday or "Dia di Rey" (
       <a href="/wiki/Koningsdag" title="Koningsdag">
        Koningsdag
       </a>
       ) is celebrated.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Iguanas_Aruba.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4272" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Iguanas_Aruba.JPG/220px-Iguanas_Aruba.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Iguanas_Aruba.JPG/330px-Iguanas_Aruba.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Iguanas_Aruba.JPG/440px-Iguanas_Aruba.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Iguanas_Aruba.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Iguana" title="Iguana">
          Iguanas
         </a>
         on a rooftop in Aruba
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Christmas and
       <a href="/wiki/New_Year%27s_Eve" title="New Year's Eve">
        New Year's Eve
       </a>
       are celebrated with the typical music and songs for
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gaita_flutes" title="Gaita flutes">
        gaitas
       </a>
       for Christmas and the Dande
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (November 2012)">
           clarification needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       for New Year, and
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Hallaca" title="Hallaca">
         ayaca
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Ponche_crema" title="Ponche crema">
         ponche crema
        </a>
       </i>
       , ham, and other typical foods and drinks. Millions of florins worth of
       <a href="/wiki/Fireworks" title="Fireworks">
        fireworks
       </a>
       are burnt at midnight on New Year's Eve. On 25 January,
       <a href="/wiki/Betico_Croes" title="Betico Croes">
        Betico Croes
       </a>
       ' birthday is celebrated.
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St_John%27s_Eve" title="St John's Eve">
        Dia di San Juan
       </a>
       is celebrated on 24 June.
      </p>
      <p>
       Besides Christmas, the religious holy days of the
       <a href="/wiki/Feast_of_the_Ascension" title="Feast of the Ascension">
        Feast of the Ascension
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Good_Friday" title="Good Friday">
        Good Friday
       </a>
       are holidays on the island.
      </p>
      <p>
       The holiday of
       <a href="/wiki/Carnival" title="Carnival">
        Carnaval
       </a>
       is also an important one in Aruba, as it is in many Caribbean and Latin American countries, and, like
       <a href="/wiki/Mardi_Gras" title="Mardi Gras">
        Mardi Gras
       </a>
       , that goes on for weeks. Its celebration in Aruba started, around the 1950s, influenced by the inhabitants from Venezuela and the nearby islands (Curaçao, St. Vincent, Trinidad, Barbados, St. Maarten and Anguilla) who came to work for the Oil refinery. Over the years the Carnival Celebration has changed and now starts from the beginning of January till the Tuesday before Ash Wednesday with a large parade on the last Sunday of the festivities (Sunday before Ash Wednesday).
      </p>
      <p>
       Tourism from the United States has recently increased the visibility of American culture on the island, with such celebrations as
       <a href="/wiki/Halloween" title="Halloween">
        Halloween
       </a>
       and Thanksgiving Day in November.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Infrastructure">
        Infrastructure
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Infrastructure">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2056" data-file-width="3648" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG/220px-Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG/330px-Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG/440px-Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aruba_Palm_Beach.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Palm Beach
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Aruba's
       <a href="/wiki/Queen_Beatrix_International_Airport" title="Queen Beatrix International Airport">
        Queen Beatrix International Airport
       </a>
       is located near Oranjestad. According to the Aruba Airport Authority, almost 1.7 million travelers used the airport in 2005, 61% of whom were Americans.
      </p>
      <p>
       Aruba has two ports, Barcadera and Playa, which are located in Oranjestad and Barcadera. The Port of Playa services all the cruise-ship lines, including
       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Caribbean_International" title="Royal Caribbean International">
        Royal Caribbean
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carnival_Cruise_Lines" title="Carnival Cruise Lines">
        Carnival Cruise Lines
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Cruise_Line" title="Norwegian Cruise Line">
        NCL
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Holland_America_Line" title="Holland America Line">
        Holland America Line
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Disney_Cruise_Line" title="Disney Cruise Line">
        Disney Cruise Line
       </a>
       and others. Nearly one million tourists enter this port per year. Aruba Ports Authority, owned and operated by the Aruban government, runs these seaports.
      </p>
      <p>
       Arubus is a government-owned bus company. Its buses operate from 3:30 a.m. until 12:30 a.m., 365 days a year. Small private vans also provide transportation services in certain areas such Hotel Area, San Nicolaas, Santa Cruz and Noord.
      </p>
      <p>
       A street car service runs on rails on the Mainstreet.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Utilities">
        Utilities
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Utilities">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Water-en Energiebedrijf Aruba, N.V. (W.E.B.) produces potable industrial water at the world's third largest desalination plant.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aruba_Hosts_International_Desalination_Conference_2007_34-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Aruba_Hosts_International_Desalination_Conference_2007-34">
         [34]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Average daily consumption in Aruba is about 37,000 long tons (38,000 t).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
        <a href="#cite_note-35">
         [35]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Communications">
        Communications
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Communications">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       There are three telecommunications providers:
       <a href="/wiki/SetarNV" title="SetarNV">
        Setar
       </a>
       , a government-based company,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mio_Wireless&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mio Wireless (page does not exist)">
        Mio Wireless
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Digicel" title="Digicel">
        Digicel
       </a>
       , both of which are privately owned. Setar is the provider of services such as internet, video conferencing,
       <a href="/wiki/GSM" title="GSM">
        GSM
       </a>
       wireless technology and land lines.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">
        <a href="#cite_note-36">
         [36]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Digicel" title="Digicel">
        Digicel
       </a>
       is Setar's competitor in wireless technology using the GSM platform, and
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mio_Wireless&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mio Wireless (page does not exist)">
        Mio Wireless
       </a>
       provides wireless technology and services using CDMA.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">
        <a href="#cite_note-37">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Places_of_interest">
        Places of interest
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Aruba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Places of interest">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1960" data-file-width="3008" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG/220px-CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG/330px-CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG/440px-CHAPEL_OF_OUR_LADY_OF_ALTO_VISTA_-_ARUBA.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">

        </div>

                        </sup>
                        <span class="wrap">
                         Became
                         <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands#Countries" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">
                          constituent countries
                         </a>
                         of the Kingdom of the Netherlands;
                         <a href="/wiki/Suriname_(Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands)" title="Suriname (Kingdom of the Netherlands)">
                          Suriname
                         </a>
                         gained
                         <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">
                          full independence
                         </a>
                         in 1975, Curaçao and Dependencies was renamed to the
                         <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Antilles" title="Netherlands Antilles">
                          Netherlands Antilles
                         </a>
                         , which was eventually dissolved in 2010.
